09/08/2023, 10:51 - Sarthak Kashmira CE 25: Regular Language Construction

Default (GPT-3.5)

User
A grammar G = (V,E, S. P) is said to be right-linear if all the productions are of the form A→Br where A, BEV and E. Similarly, a grammar is said to be left-linear if all the productions are of the form A Brir. Let G (V, E, S, Pi) be right-linear and G₂ (V2, E. S2, P2) be left-linear grammar, = and assume that V and V2 are disjoint. Consider a new grammar Gnew (S) UVUV, E. SP), where S VUV and P (S→ = SS2) UPU P2. Show that L(Gnew) is regular.

ChatGPT
To show that the language generated by the grammar Gnew (S, V, E, P) is regular, we need to demonstrate that it can be recognized by a finite automaton or expressed using a regular expression.

The grammar Gnew consists of non-terminals S, U, V, V2 and productions:

S → UVUV
U → SS2
V → E
V2 → E
Let's break down the steps to show that L(Gnew) is regular:

The production S → UVUV means that any string generated by S can be divided into two parts, each generated by U and VUV, respectively. This suggests a non-deterministic finite automaton (NFA) could simulate this by transitioning between states representing U and VUV.

The production U → SS2 indicates that U generates strings by concatenating two substrings generated by S and S2. This is a regular operation, as regular languages are closed under concatenation.

The productions V → E and V2 → E mean that both V and V2 can be replaced by the empty string. This is again a regular operation, as regular languages are closed under the empty string operation.

Finally, the production S → UVUV implies that the language generated by Gnew is a combination of the operations described above, all of which are regular. Since regular languages are closed under the operations of concatenation, union, and closure, we can conclude that L(Gnew) is regular.

In summary, by breaking down the grammar's productions and operations, we can see that each step involves regular operations, and thus the language generated by Gnew is regular.

09/08/2023, 10:54 - Sarthak Kashmira CE 25: Regular languages nor operation

Default (GPT-3.5)

User
The nor (4) of two languages is defined as
+(L1,L2) = {w: w Ly and we L2}-
Show that the family of regular languages is closed under the nor (4) operation.

ChatGPT
To show that the family of regular languages is closed under the nor (4) operation, we need to demonstrate that if L1 and L2 are regular languages, then +(L1, L2) is also a regular language.

One way to approach this is by using regular expressions and finite automata. Let's denote the regular expressions for L1 and L2 as r1 and r2, respectively. Then, we can construct a regular expression for +(L1, L2) as follows:

Regular expression for +(L1, L2) = r1 * (Σ - r2) *

Here, r1 * represents zero or more repetitions of strings generated by r1, and (Σ - r2) * represents zero or more repetitions of strings over the alphabet Σ (the set of all possible symbols) excluding those generated by r2.

This regular expression represents the language where any string from L1 is concatenated with any string that is not in L2, allowing us to achieve the nor (4) operation.

Since regular expressions can be converted into finite automata, this demonstrates that the family of regular languages is closed under the nor (4) operation.

09/08/2023, 11:18 - Vedansh CE: 1(a) --> The grammar produces language of all strings of a's and b's that have same number of a's and b's. Proof - First, let’s prove that any string generated by this grammar has the same number of a’s and b’s. We can do this by induction on the number of derivation steps.
Base case: The string epsilon can be generated in one derivation step by applying the production rule S -> epsilon. This string has 0 a’s and 0 b’s, so it has the same number of a’s and b’s.
Inductive step: Assume that any string that can be generated in n derivation steps has the same number of a’s and b’s. We need to show that any string that can be generated in n+1 derivation steps also has the same number of a’s and b’s.
If the last production rule applied is S -> SS, then the generated string is a concatenation of two strings, each of which can be generated in at most n derivation steps. By the induction hypothesis, each of these strings has the same number of a’s and b’s, so their concatenation also has the same number of a’s and b’s.
If the last production rule applied is either S -> aSb or S -> bSa, then the generated string has one more a and one more b than the string generated by applying the production rule to S. Since this string can be generated in at most n derivation steps, it has the same number of a’s and b’s by the induction hypothesis. Therefore, adding one more a and one more b to it results in a string that also has the same number of a’s and b’s.
Next, let’s prove that any string of a’s and b’s that has the same number of a’s and b’s can be generated by this grammar. We can do this by induction on the length of the string.
Base case: The empty string can be generated by applying the production rule S -> epsilon.
Inductive step: Assume that any string of length n that has the same number of a’s and b’s can be generated by this grammar. We need to show that any string of length n+2 that has the same number of a’s and b’s can also be generated by this grammar.
If the first character is an ‘a’, then there must exist an index i such that characters 2 through i form a substring with one more ‘b’ than ‘a’, and characters i+1 through n+2 form a substring with one more ‘a’ than ‘b’. By induction hypothesis, both substrings can be derived from S. Therefore, we can derive the whole string from S by first applying S -> aSb, then deriving characters 2 through i from first S, and characters i+1 through n+2 from second S.
If the first character is a ‘b’, then we can use similar reasoning as above but apply S -> bSa instead.

09/08/2023, 11:44 - Amritansh Gupta CE: Step 1: Context-Free Grammar for Palindromes
A context-free grammar G1 for generating palindromes can be given as follows:

Copy code
S -> aSa | bSb | a | b | ε
This grammar generates palindromes over the alphabet {a, b}.

Step 2: Modify Grammar for Complement
To generate the complement of palindromes, we can modify the grammar G1 as follows:

Copy code
S -> X | aSa | bSb | a | b | ε
X -> aX | bX | Y
Y -> aY | bY | Z
Z -> aZ | bZ | ε
In the modified grammar G2, the non-terminal S generates strings that are not palindromes. The production S -> X allows for strings that are not palindromes. The non-terminals X, Y, and Z are used to generate arbitrary strings of 'a' and 'b'. This modification ensures that the grammar generates the complement of palindromes.

Therefore, the complement of the language L(G) = {wwR : w ∈ {a, b}*} is context-free, where the modifications made to the palindrome grammar result in a grammar generating the complement of palindromes.

03/11/2023, 10:52 - Piyush Nayak: 2
Certainly! You can create a parent and child process in C using the `fork` system call. Here's a simple C program that demonstrates this:

```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <sys/types.h>

int main() {
    pid_t child_pid;

    // Create a child process
    child_pid = fork();

    if (child_pid < 0) {
        perror("Fork failed");
        exit(1);
    }

    if (child_pid == 0) {
        // This code is executed by the child process
        printf("Child process (PID: %d) is running.\n", getpid());
    } else {
        // This code is executed by the parent process
        printf("Parent process (PID: %d) created a child process with PID: %d.\n", getpid(), child_pid);
    }

    return 0;
}
```

In this program:

1. The `fork` system call is used to create a child process. The parent process receives the child's PID, and the child process receives 0 as the return value.

2. The parent process prints its PID and the child's PID, while the child process prints its own PID.

When you run this program, it will create a parent process and a child process, and each process will print its PID. The child process is a copy of the parent process, so they both execute the same code but have different PIDs.
03/11/2023, 10:52 - Piyush Nayak: 3
You can create a parent and child process in C where the child process sleeps for 10 seconds, and the parent process waits for the child to complete using the `fork` and `wait` system calls. Here's a C program that accomplishes this:

```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#include <sys/wait.h>

int main() {
    pid_t child_pid;

    // Create a child process
    child_pid = fork();

    if (child_pid < 0) {
        perror("Fork failed");
        exit(1);
    }

    if (child_pid == 0) {
        // This code is executed by the child process
        printf("Child process (PID: %d) is sleeping for 10 seconds...\n", getpid());
        sleep(10);
        printf("Child process (PID: %d) is done.\n", getpid());
    } else {
        // This code is executed by the parent process
        printf("Parent process (PID: %d) is waiting for the child process (PID: %d) to complete...\n", getpid(), child_pid);
        wait(NULL); // Parent waits for any child process to complete
        printf("Parent process (PID: %d) is done.\n", getpid());
    }

    return 0;
}
```

In this C program:

1. The `fork` system call is used to create a child process, similar to the previous example.

2. The child process sleeps for 10 seconds using `sleep(10)` to simulate a delay.

3. The parent process waits for the child process to complete using `wait(NULL)`. This will make the parent wait until any child process terminates.

4. Both the parent and child processes print their PIDs, and the parent prints messages to indicate the waiting and completion steps.

When you run this program, it will create a parent process and a child process. The child process will sleep for 10 seconds, and the parent process will wait for the child to complete before it finishes.

06/11/2023, 14:09 - UMAKANT SINGH: import java.io.File;

public class CountFilesAndSubdirectories {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        // Specify the directory path
        String directoryPath = "/path/to/your/directory";
        
        // Create a File object for the specified directory
        File directory = new File(directoryPath);
        
        // Check if the specified path is a directory
        if (directory.isDirectory()) {
            int fileCount = 0;
            int subdirectoryCount = 0;
            
            // Get list of files and directories in the directory
            File[] filesAndDirectories = directory.listFiles();
            
            // Iterate through the files and directories and count files and subdirectories
            if (filesAndDirectories != null) {
                for (File fileOrDir : filesAndDirectories) {
                    if (fileOrDir.isFile()) {
                        fileCount++;
                    } else if (fileOrDir.isDirectory()) {
                        subdirectoryCount++;
                    }
                }
                
                // Print the counts
                System.out.println("Number of files: " + fileCount);
                System.out.println("Number of subdirectories: " + subdirectoryCount);
            } else {
                System.out.println("Error: Unable to list files and directories in the specified directory.");
            }
        } else {
            System.out.println("Error: Specified path is not a directory.");
        }
    }
}

import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Set;

public class CountDistinctFiles {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        // Specify the directory path
        String directoryPath = "/path/to/your/directory";
        
        // Create a File object for the specified directory
        File directory = new File(directoryPath);
        
        // Check if the specified path is a directory
        if (directory.isDirectory()) {
            // Create a set to store distinct file names
            Set<String> fileNames = new HashSet<>();
            
            // Get list of files in the directory
            File[] files = directory.listFiles();
            
            // Iterate through the files and add their names to the set
            if (files != null) {
                for (File file : files) {
                    if (file.isFile()) {
                        fileNames.add(file.getName());
                    }
                }
                
                // Print the number of distinct files
                System.out.println("Number of distinct files: " + fileNames.size());
            } else {
                System.out.println("Error: Unable to list files in the specified directory.");
            }
        } else {
            System.out.println("Error: Specified path is not a directory.");
        }
    }
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		for(int i=0;i<t;i++){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    int x=sc.nextInt();
		    int y=sc.nextInt();
		    int[] arr=new int[n];
		    int cop=x;
		    int ncop=0;
		    for(int j=0;j<n;j++){
		        arr[j]=sc.nextInt();
		        ncop+=arr[j];
		        cop+=(arr[j]-y>0?arr[j]-y:0);
		    }
		    if(cop<ncop)
		      System.out.println("COUPON");
		    else 
		      System.out.println("NO COUPON");
		}
	}
}

class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		for(int i=0;i<t;i++){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    int[] a=new int[n];
		    int[] b=new int[n];
		    int currstr=0,maxstr=0;
		    for(int j=0;j<n;j++)
		      a[j]=sc.nextInt();
		    for(int j=0;j<n;j++)
		      b[j]=sc.nextInt();
		    for(int j=0;j<n;j++){
		        if(a[j]>0 && b[j]>0)currstr+=1;
		        else currstr=0;
		          maxstr=maxstr>currstr?maxstr:currstr;
		    }        
		    System.out.println(maxstr);
		        
		}
	}
}

class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		for(int i=0;i<t;i++){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    String s=sc.next();
		    String ans="";
		    for(int j=0;j<n-1;j+=2){
		        if(s.charAt(j)=='0' && s.charAt(j+1)=='0')
		          ans+='A';
		        else if(s.charAt(j)=='0' && s.charAt(j+1)=='1')
		           ans+='T';
		        else if(s.charAt(j)=='1' && s.charAt(j+1)=='0')
		          ans+='C';
		        else  ans+='G';    
		    }
		    System.out.println(ans);
		}
	}
}

{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		for(int i=0;i<t;i++){
		    String s1=sc.next();
		    String s2=sc.next();
		    int n=s1.length();
		    int m=s2.length();
		    if(n!=m)
		      System.out.println("No");
		    else{
		        int flag=0;
		        for(int j=0;j<n;j++){
		            if(s1.charAt(j)=='?'||s2.charAt(j)=='?'||s1.charAt(j)==s2.charAt(j))
		                continue;
		            else{
		                flag=1;
		                break;
		            }      
		        }
		        if(flag==0)
		           System.out.println("Yes");
		        else  System.out.println("No");     
		    }    
		}
	}
}

class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		for(int i=0;i<t;i++){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    String str=sc.next();
		    int s=0;//s=0 means a is server s=1 means b is server
		    int p1=0,p2=0;
		    for(int j=0;j<n;j++){
		        char c=str.charAt(j);
		        if(s==0 && c=='A')p1+=1;
		        else if(s==0 && c=='B')s=1;
		        else if(s==1 && c=='B')p2+=1;
		        else  s=0;
		    }
		    System.out.println(p1+" "+p2);
		}
	}
}

	{

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
    public static class Post {
        int friendId;
        int popularity;
        String content;

        public Post(int friendId, int popularity, String content) {
            this.friendId = friendId;
            this.popularity = popularity;
            this.content = content;
        }
    }

    public static List<Post> orderPosts(List<Integer> specialFriends, List<Post> posts) {
        Collections.sort(posts, (post1, post2) -> {
            if (specialFriends.contains(post1.friendId) && specialFriends.contains(post2.friendId)) {
                return Integer.compare(post2.popularity, post1.popularity);
            } else if (specialFriends.contains(post1.friendId)) {
                return -1;
            } else if (specialFriends.contains(post2.friendId)) {
                return 1;
            } else {
                return Integer.compare(post2.popularity, post1.popularity);
            }
        });

        return posts;
    }
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int n=sc.nextInt();
		int m=sc.nextInt();
		int[] spec=new int[n];
		int[] f=new int[m];
		int[] p=new int[m];
		String[] s=new String[m];
		List<Integer> specialFriends = new ArrayList<>();
		for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
		    spec[i]=sc.nextInt();
		    specialFriends.add(spec[i]);
		}
		List<Post> posts = new ArrayList<>();
		for(int i=0;i<m;i++){
		    f[i]=sc.nextInt();
		    p[i]=sc.nextInt();
		    s[i]=sc.next();
		    posts.add(new Post(f[i],p[i],s[i]));
		}  
	    List<Post> orderedPosts = orderPosts(specialFriends, posts);
        for (Post post : orderedPosts) {
            System.out.println(post.content);
        }	
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
    public static int findMostPopularPost(int[] likes, int[] comments) {
        int mostPopularPostIndex = 0;
        int maxLikes = likes[0];
        int maxComments = comments[0];

        for (int i = 1; i < likes.length; i++) {
            if (likes[i] > maxLikes || (likes[i] == maxLikes && comments[i] > maxComments)) {
                mostPopularPostIndex = i;
                maxLikes = likes[i];
                maxComments = comments[i];
            }
        }

        return mostPopularPostIndex;
    }
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		while(t-->0){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    int[] a=new int[n];
		    int[] b=new int[n];
		    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)a[i]=sc.nextInt();
		    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)b[i]=sc.nextInt();
		    int mpind = findMostPopularPost(a,b);
		    System.out.println(mpind+1);
		}
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		while(t-->0){
		   int n=sc.nextInt();
		   int[] arr=new int[n];
		   for(int i=0;i<n;i++)arr[i]=sc.nextInt();
           System.out.println(getFactorCount(arr));
		}
	}
	public static int getFactorCount(int[] nums) {
        Map<Integer, Integer> primeCounts = new HashMap<>();

        for (int num : nums) {
            int i = 2;
            while (i * i <= num) {
                if (num % i == 0) {
                    num /= i;
                    primeCounts.put(i, primeCounts.getOrDefault(i, 0) + 1);
                } else {
                    i++;
                }
            }
            if (num > 1) {
                primeCounts.put(num, primeCounts.getOrDefault(num, 0) + 1);
            }
        }

        int factorCount = 1;
        for (int count : primeCounts.values()) {
            factorCount *= count + 1;
        }

        return factorCount;
    }
	
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		while(t-->0){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    int[] arr=new int[n];
		    HashMap<Integer,Integer> hm=new HashMap<>();
		    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
		        arr[i]=sc.nextInt();
		        int f=hm.getOrDefault(arr[i],0);
		        hm.put(arr[i],f+1);
		    }
		    int maxelem=arr[0];
		    int freq=0;
		    boolean ans=false;
		    for(Map.Entry<Integer,Integer> map:hm.entrySet()){
		        if(map.getValue()>freq){
		            freq=map.getValue();
		            maxelem=map.getKey();
		            ans=true;
		        }
		        else if(map.getValue()==freq){
		            ans=false;
		        }
		    }
		    if(ans==true)
		      System.out.println("YES");
		    else System.out.println("NO");
		}
	}
	
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		while(t-->0){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    int m=sc.nextInt();
		    int[] p=new int[m];
		    for(int i=0;i<m;i++)p[i]=sc.nextInt();
		    ArrayList<ArrayList<Integer>> l=new ArrayList<>();
		    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
		        int c=sc.nextInt();
		        ArrayList<Integer> l1=new ArrayList<>();
		        for(int j=0;j<c;j++){
		           l1.add(sc.nextInt()); 
		        }
		        Collections.sort(l1,Collections.reverseOrder());
		        l.add(l1);
		    }
		    int ans=0;
		    for(int i=0;i<m;i++){
		        ArrayList<Integer> l1=l.get(p[i]);
		        if(l1.size()>0){
		            ans+=l1.get(0);
		            l1.remove(0);
		        }
		    }
		    System.out.println(ans);
		}
	}
}

	       int n=sc.nextInt();
	       int[] arr=new int[n];
	       int maxf=0;
	       HashMap<Integer,Integer> hm=new HashMap<>();
	       for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
	           arr[i]=sc.nextInt();
	           int x=hm.getOrDefault(arr[i],0);
	           hm.put(arr[i],x+1);
	           maxf=Math.max(maxf,x+1);
	       }
	       System.out.println(n-maxf);
	   }
	}

class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		while(t-->0){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    int k=sc.nextInt();
		    int[] arr=new int[n];
		    long sum=0,kid=0,parent=0;
		    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
		        arr[i]=sc.nextInt();
		        sum+=(long)arr[i];
		    }
		    Arrays.sort(arr);
		    for(int i=0;i<k;i++){
		        kid+=arr[i];
		        parent+=arr[n-i-1];
		    }
		    System.out.println(Math.max(sum-2*kid,2*parent-sum));
		}
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
	Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        
        long t = scanner.nextLong();
        
        while (t-- > 0) {
            long n = scanner.nextLong();
            long m = scanner.nextLong();
            long h = scanner.nextLong();
            
            long[] c = new long[(int) n];
            long[] o = new long[(int) m];
            
            for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
                c[i] = scanner.nextLong();
            
            for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
                o[i] = scanner.nextLong();
            
            Arrays.sort(c);
            Arrays.sort(o);
            
            long cEnd = n - 1;
            long oEnd = m - 1;
            long answer1 = 0;
            
            while (cEnd >= 0 && oEnd >= 0) {
                long capacity = c[(int) cEnd];
                long outlerCap = o[(int) oEnd];
                answer1 += Math.min(capacity, h * outlerCap);
                cEnd--;
                oEnd--;
            }
            
            cEnd = 0;
            oEnd = 0;
            long answer2 = 0;
            
            while (cEnd < n && oEnd < m) {
                long capacity = c[(int) cEnd];
                long outlerCap = o[(int) oEnd];
                answer2 += Math.min(capacity, h * outlerCap);
                cEnd++;
                oEnd++;
            }
            
            System.out.println(Math.max(answer1, answer2));
        }
        
	}
}

	{

		int t = sc.nextInt();

		{
		    String s = sc.next();
		    int sn=0,mo=0, co=0;
		    for(int i=0; i<s.length(); i++)
		    {
		        if(s.charAt(i)=='s')
		            sn++;
		        else if(s.charAt(i)=='m')
		            mo++;
		    }
		    for(int i=0;i<s.length()-1;i++)
		    {
		        if(s.charAt(i)!=s.charAt(i+1)){
		            co++;
		        i++;}
		    }
		    sn=sn-co;
		    if(mo>sn)
		        System.out.println("mongooses");
		    else if(mo==sn)
		        System.out.println("tie");
		    else
		        System.out.println("snakes");
		}
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
	    InputStreamReader in = new InputStreamReader (System.in);
	BufferedReader br = new BufferedReader(in);		
        int T = Integer.parseInt(br.readLine());               
        for (int i=0; i<T; i++)
        {
            int N = Integer.parseInt(br.readLine());   
            int len = N*N;
            int[] arr = new int[len];
            for (int j=0; j<N; j++)
            {
                String[] A = br.readLine().split(" ");
                for (int k=0; k<N; k++)
                    arr[j*N+k] = Integer.parseInt(A[k]);
            }
            long total = 0;
            int max = 0;
            for (int j=len-N; j<len; j++)
            {
                if (arr[j] > max)
                    max = arr[j];
            }
            total += (long) max;
            int maxI = 0;
            for (int j=N-2; j>=0; j--)
            {
                maxI = 0;
                int start = j*N;
                int end = (j+1)*N;
                for (int k=start; k<end; k++)
                {
                    if (arr[k] > maxI && arr[k] < max)
                        maxI = arr[k];
                }
                if (maxI == 0)
                {
                    total = -1;
                    break;
                }
                else 
                {
                    total += (long) maxI;
                    max = maxI;
                }
            }
            System.out.println(total);
        }        
        br.close();
    }
}

           long s=1,e=n;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		while(t-->0){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    int h=sc.nextInt();
		    int[] arr=new int[n];
		    int max=0;
		    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
		        arr[i]=sc.nextInt();
		        max=max>arr[i]?max:arr[i];
		    }
		    int s=1,e=max;
		    int ans=max;
		    while(s<=e){
		        int mid=s+(e-s)/2;
		        if(time(arr,mid)<=h){
		            ans=mid;
		            e=mid-1;
		        }
		        else s=mid+1;
		    }
		    System.out.println(ans);
		}
	    
	}
	public static int time(int[] arr,int speed){
	   int h=0;
	   for(int i=0;i<arr.length;i++){
		  h+=arr[i]/speed;
		  if(arr[i]%speed!=0)h+=1;
	   }
	   return h;
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		FastReader in = new FastReader();
		int T = in.nextInt();
		for(int i=0; i<T; i++) {
			int N = in.nextInt();
			double v = 0;
			int best = 0;
			for(int j=0; j<N; j++) {
				v += in.nextInt();
				double a = v/(j+1);
				if((int) Math.ceil(v/(j+1)) > best)
						best = (int) Math.ceil(v/(j+1));
			}
			System.out.println(best);
		}
	}

class FastReader {
    BufferedReader br;
    StringTokenizer st;

    public FastReader()
    {
        br = new BufferedReader(
            new InputStreamReader(System.in));
    }
    
    public FastReader(File file) throws FileNotFoundException
    {
        br = new BufferedReader(
            new FileReader(file));
    }

    public String next()
    {
        while (st == null || !st.hasMoreElements()) {
            try {
                st = new StringTokenizer(br.readLine());
            }
            catch (IOException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }
        }
        return st.nextToken();
    }

    public int nextInt() { return Integer.parseInt(next()); }
    
    public int[] nextIntArray(int n) { 
    	int[] r = new int[n];
    	for(int i=0; i<n; i++) {
    		r[i] = Integer.parseInt(next());
    	}
    	return r;
    }

    public long nextLong() { return Long.parseLong(next()); }
    
    public long[] nextLongArray(int n) { 
    	long[] r = new long[n];
    	for(int i=0; i<n; i++) {
    		r[i] = Long.parseLong(next());
    	}
    	return r;
    }

    public double nextDouble()
    {
        return Double.parseDouble(next());
    }

    public String nextLine()
    {
        String str = "";
        try {
            if(st.hasMoreTokens()){
                str = st.nextToken("\n");
            }
            else{
                str = br.readLine();
            }
        }
        catch (IOException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
        return str;
    }
    
    public boolean hasNext() throws IOException {
    	return br.ready();
    }
}

class ArrayUtil {
	
	public static long[] max(long[] array, long initial_value) {
		int n = array.length;
		long max = initial_value;
		long index = -1;
		for(int i=0; i<n; i++) {
			if(array[i] > max) {
				max = array[i];
				index = i;
			}
		}
		return new long[] {max, index};
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
    static final StdIn in = new StdIn();
	static final PrintWriter out = new PrintWriter(System.out);
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		long m=in.nextLong();
		int n=in.nextInt();
		long[] l = new long[n], r = new long[n];
		for(int i=0; i<n; ++i) {
			l[i]=in.nextLong();
			r[i]=in.nextLong();
		}
		long lb=1, rb=m/n;
		while(lb<=rb) {
			long mb=(lb+rb)/2;
			long a=0;
			for(int i=0; i<n; ++i)
				a=Math.max(l[i]-i*mb, a);
			boolean ok=true;
			long lp=n*mb+a;
			for(int i=n-1; i>=0&&ok; --i) {
				lp=Math.min(r[i], lp-mb);
				ok=l[i]<=lp;
			}
//			out.println(mb+" "+lp);
			ok&=lp+m-((n-1)*mb+a)>=mb;
			if(ok)
				lb=mb+1;
			else
				rb=mb-1;
		}
		out.println(rb);
		out.close();
	}
	
	static class StdIn {
		final private int BUFFER_SIZE = 1 << 16;
		private DataInputStream din;
		private byte[] buffer;
		private int bufferPointer, bytesRead;
		public StdIn() {
			din = new DataInputStream(System.in);
			buffer = new byte[BUFFER_SIZE];
			bufferPointer = bytesRead = 0;
		}
		public StdIn(InputStream in) {
			try{
				din = new DataInputStream(in);
			} catch(Exception e) {
				throw new RuntimeException();
			}
			buffer = new byte[BUFFER_SIZE];
			bufferPointer = bytesRead = 0;
		}
		public String next() {
			int c;
			while((c=read())!=-1&&(c==' '||c=='\n'||c=='\r'));
			StringBuilder s = new StringBuilder();
			while (c != -1)
			{
				if (c == ' ' || c == '\n'||c=='\r')
					break;
				s.append((char)c);
				c=read();
			}
			return s.toString();
		}
		public String nextLine() {
			int c;
			while((c=read())!=-1&&(c==' '||c=='\n'||c=='\r'));
			StringBuilder s = new StringBuilder();
			while (c != -1)
			{
				if (c == '\n'||c=='\r')
					break;
				s.append((char)c);
				c = read();
			}
			return s.toString();
		}
		public int nextInt() {
			int ret = 0;
			byte c = read();
			while (c <= ' ')
				c = read();
			boolean neg = (c == '-');
			if (neg)
				c = read();
			do
				ret = ret * 10 + c - '0';
			while ((c = read()) >= '0' && c <= '9');

			if (neg)
				return -ret;
			return ret;
		}
		public int[] readIntArray(int n, int os) {
			int[] ar = new int[n];
			for(int i=0; i<n; ++i)
				ar[i]=nextInt()+os;
			return ar;
		}
		public long nextLong() {
			long ret = 0;
			byte c = read();
			while (c <= ' ')
				c = read();
			boolean neg = (c == '-');
			if (neg)
				c = read();
			do
				ret = ret * 10 + c - '0';
			while ((c = read()) >= '0' && c <= '9');
			if (neg)
				return -ret;
			return ret;
		}
		public long[] readLongArray(int n, long os) {
			long[] ar = new long[n];
			for(int i=0; i<n; ++i)
				ar[i]=nextLong()+os;
			return ar;
		}
		public double nextDouble() {
			double ret = 0, div = 1;
			byte c = read();
			while (c <= ' ')
				c = read();
			boolean neg = (c == '-');
			if (neg)
				c = read();
			do
				ret = ret * 10 + c - '0';
			while ((c = read()) >= '0' && c <= '9');
			if (c == '.')
				while ((c = read()) >= '0' && c <= '9')
					ret += (c - '0') / (div *= 10);
			if (neg)
				return -ret;
			return ret;
		}
		private void fillBuffer() throws IOException {
			bytesRead = din.read(buffer, bufferPointer = 0, BUFFER_SIZE);
			if (bytesRead == -1)
				buffer[0] = -1;
		}
		private byte read() {
			try{
				if (bufferPointer == bytesRead)
					fillBuffer();
				return buffer[bufferPointer++];
			} catch(IOException e) {
				throw new RuntimeException();
			}
		}
		public void close() throws IOException {
			if (din == null)
				return;
			din.close();
		}
	}
}

		    int[] dp=new int[n];

		        if(Integer.signum(arr[i+1])!=Integer.signum(arr[i]))dp[i]=dp[i+1]+1;
		        else dp[i]=1;
		    }

		    System.out.println();
		}
	}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		while(t-->0){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    long[][] dp=new long[n][n];
		    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
		        for(int j=0;j<=i;j++){
		            dp[i][j]=sc.nextLong();
		        }
		    }
		    for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
		        for(int j=0;j<=i;j++){
		            if(j==0)dp[i][j]=dp[i-1][j]+dp[i][j];
		            else if(i==j)dp[i][j]=dp[i-1][j-1]+dp[i][j];
		            else dp[i][j]=Math.max(dp[i-1][j-1],dp[i-1][j])+dp[i][j];
		        }
		    }
		    long max=dp[n-1][0];
		    for(int i=1;i<n;i++)
		        max=max>dp[n-1][i]?max:dp[n-1][i];
		    System.out.println(max);
		}
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		int n,linear,l_start=0,l_end=0,l_flag=0,diag1,diag_start1=0,diag_end1=0,diag_flag1=0;
        int diag2,diag_start2=0,diag_end2=0,diag_flag2=0;
        char [][] A;
        int [][] H, V, D1, D2;

        BufferedReader br=new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        n= Integer.parseInt(br.readLine());

        A= new char[n][n];
        H= new int[n][n];
        V= new int[n][n];
        D1= new int[n][n];
        D2= new int[n][n];


        for(int i=0;i<n; i++)
        {
            String str= br.readLine();

            linear=0;
            l_flag=0;
            for(int j=0; j<n; j++)
            {
                A[i][j]=str.charAt(j);

                if(A[i][j]=='X')
                {
                    H[i][j]=1;

                    if((j-1>=0) && (A[i][j-1]=='X'))
                    {
                        l_flag=1;
                        linear++;
                    }

                    if(l_flag==0)
                    {
                        l_start=j;
                        linear=1;
                    }

                }
                else
                {
                    if(l_flag==1)
                        l_end=j-1;
                    else
                        l_end=l_start;

                    H[i][j]=0;
                    l_flag=0;
                }

                if((j==n-1) && (A[i][j]=='X'))
                {
                    l_end=j;
                }

                if( l_start-l_end!=0)
                {
                    for(int k=l_start;k<=l_end;k++)
                    {
                        H[i][k]=linear;
                    }

                }
            }
        }


        for (int i = 0; i < 2 * n - 1; ++i)
        {
            diag1=0;

             diag2=0;
            int z = i < n ? 0 : i - n + 1;

            diag_end1=diag_start1=z;
            diag_end2=diag_start2=z;

            for (int j = z; j <= i - z; ++j)
            {
                if(A[j][i - j]=='X')
                {
                    D1[j][i - j]=1;

                    if((j-1>=z) && (A[j-1][i - j+1]=='X'))
                    {
                        diag_flag1=1;
                        diag1++;
                    }

                    if(diag_flag1==0)
                    {
                        diag_start1=j;
                        diag1=1;
                    }

                }
                else if(A[j][i - j]!='X')
                {
                    if(diag_flag1==1)
                    {
                        diag_end1=j-1;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        diag_end1=-1;
                    }
                    D1[j][i - j]=0;
                    diag_flag1=0;
                }


                if((j==i-z) && (A[j][i - j]=='X'))
                {
                    diag_end1=j;
                    diag_flag1=0;
                }

                if( diag_start1!=diag_end1 && diag_end1!=-1)
                {

                    for(int k=diag_start1;k<=diag_end1;k++)
                    {
                        D1[k][i-k]=diag1;
                    }
                }


                if(A[j][(n-1)-(i-j)]=='X')
                {
                    D2[j][(n-1)-(i-j)]=1;

                    if((j-1>=z) && (A[j-1][(n-1)-(i-j+1)]=='X'))
                    {
                        diag_flag2=1;
                        ++diag2;
                    }

                    if(diag_flag2==0)
                    {
                        diag_start2=j;
                        diag2=1;
                    }

                }
                else if(A[j][(n-1)-(i-j)]!='X')
                {
                    if(diag_flag2==1)
                    {
                        diag_end2=j-1;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        diag_end2=-1;
                    }
                    D2[j][(n-1)-(i-j)]=0;
                    diag_flag2=0;
                }


                if((j==i-z) && (A[j][(n-1)-(i-j)]=='X'))
                {
                    diag_end2=j;
                    diag_flag2=0;
                }

                if( diag_start2!=diag_end2 && diag_end2!=-1)
                {

                    for(int k=diag_start2;k<=diag_end2;k++)
                    {
                        D2[k][(n-1)-(i-k)]=diag2;

                    }
                }

            }

        }


        for(int i=0;i<n; i++)
        {

            linear=0;
            l_flag=0;
            l_start=l_end=-1;
            for(int j=0; j<n; j++)
            {
                if(D1[i][j]<D2[i][j])
                {
                    D1[i][j]=D2[i][j];
                }

                if(A[j][i]=='X')
                {
                    V[j][i]=1;

                    if((j-1>=0) && (A[j-1][i]=='X'))
                    {
                        l_flag=1;
                        linear++;
                    }

                    if(l_flag==0)
                    {
                        l_start=j;
                        linear=1;
                    }

                }
                else
                {
                    if(l_flag==1)
                        l_end=j-1;
                    else
                        l_end=l_start;

                    V[j][i]=0;
                    l_flag=0;
                }

                if((j==n-1) && (A[j][i]=='X'))
                {
                    l_end=j;
                }

                if( l_start-l_end!=0)
                {
                    for(int k=l_start;k<=l_end;k++)
                    {
                        V[k][i]=linear;
                    }

                }
            }
        }



        StringBuffer sb=new StringBuffer("");
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
        {
            for(int j=0;j<n;j++)
            {
                sb.append((H[i][j]>V[i][j])?(H[i][j]>D1[i][j]?H[i][j]:D1[i][j]):(V[i][j]>D1[i][j]?V[i][j]:D1[i][j]));
                sb.append(" ");
            }

            sb.append("\n");
        }
        System.out.println(sb);
    }

}

08/11/2023, 22:00 - Badal CE: /* package codechef; // don't place package name! */

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	static String KNIGHT = "K";
    static Character PAWN = 'P';
    static Integer BOARD_SIZE;

    static int[][] BLACK_PAWNS_CAPTURED;

    static class KnightPosition {
        private int row;
        private int column;

        public KnightPosition(int row, int column) {
            this.row = row;
            this.column = column;
        }

        public int getRow() {
            return row;
        }

        public void setRow(int row) {
            this.row = row;
        }

        public int getColumn() {
            return column;
        }

        public void setColumn(int column) {
            this.column = column;
        }

    }

    private static KnightPosition getKnightPosition(List<String> chessBoard) throws Exception {
        for(int i = 0; i < BOARD_SIZE; i++) {
            if(chessBoard.get(i).contains(KNIGHT)) {
                return new KnightPosition(i, chessBoard.get(i).indexOf(KNIGHT));
            }
        }
        throw new Exception("Knight not found.");
    }

    private static int maximumBlackPawnsCaptured(List<String> chessBoard,
                                                 KnightPosition knightPosition) {
        int count = 0;
        if(!((knightPosition.getRow() > -1 && knightPosition.getRow() < BOARD_SIZE)
                && (knightPosition.getColumn() > -1 && knightPosition.getColumn() < BOARD_SIZE))) {
            return count;
        }
        if(BLACK_PAWNS_CAPTURED[knightPosition.getRow()][knightPosition.getColumn()] > -1) {
            return BLACK_PAWNS_CAPTURED[knightPosition.getRow()][knightPosition.getColumn()];
        }
        if(chessBoard.get(knightPosition.getRow()).charAt(knightPosition.getColumn()) == PAWN) {
            count++;
        }
        count += Math.max(
                Math.max(maximumBlackPawnsCaptured(chessBoard, new KnightPosition(knightPosition.getRow() - 2, knightPosition.getColumn() + 1)),
                        maximumBlackPawnsCaptured(chessBoard, new KnightPosition(knightPosition.getRow() - 1, knightPosition.getColumn() + 2))),
                Math.max(maximumBlackPawnsCaptured(chessBoard, new KnightPosition(knightPosition.getRow() + 1, knightPosition.getColumn() + 2)),
                        maximumBlackPawnsCaptured(chessBoard, new KnightPosition(knightPosition.getRow() + 2, knightPosition.getColumn() + 1))));
        BLACK_PAWNS_CAPTURED[knightPosition.getRow()][knightPosition.getColumn()] = count;
        return count;
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
    {
        FastReader fastReader = new FastReader();

        int testCases = fastReader.nextInt();
        while(testCases-- > 0) {
            BOARD_SIZE = fastReader.nextInt();
            BLACK_PAWNS_CAPTURED = new int[BOARD_SIZE][BOARD_SIZE];
            int n = BOARD_SIZE;
            List<String> chessBoard = new ArrayList<>();
            while(n-- > 0) {
                chessBoard.add(fastReader.nextLine());
            }
            for(int i=0; i<BOARD_SIZE; i++) {
                for(int j=0; j<BOARD_SIZE; j++) {
                    BLACK_PAWNS_CAPTURED[i][j] = -1;
                }
            }
            KnightPosition knightPosition = getKnightPosition(chessBoard);
            System.out.println(maximumBlackPawnsCaptured(chessBoard, knightPosition));
        }

    }

    static class FastReader {
        BufferedReader br;
        StringTokenizer st;

        public FastReader()
        {
            br = new BufferedReader(
                    new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        }

        String next()
        {
            while (st == null || !st.hasMoreElements()) {
                try {
                    st = new StringTokenizer(br.readLine());
                }
                catch (IOException e) {
                    e.printStackTrace();
                }
            }
            return st.nextToken();
        }

        int nextInt() { return Integer.parseInt(next()); }

        long nextLong() { return Long.parseLong(next()); }

        double nextDouble()
        {
            return Double.parseDouble(next());
        }

        String nextLine()
        {
            String str = "";
            try {
                if(st.hasMoreTokens()){
                    str = st.nextToken("\n");
                }
                else{
                    str = br.readLine();
                }
            }
            catch (IOException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }
            return str;
        }
    }
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
    static List<Integer> convertToArrayList( int a [] ){
        
        List<Integer> ans = new ArrayList<>();
        
        for( int e : a ){
            ans.add( e );
        }
        
        return ans;
    }
    
    static void swap( int [] a , int l , int r ){
        
        int temp = a[l];
        a[l] = a[r];
        a[r] = temp;
        
    }
    
    static void permute( int l , int n , int [] a , HashSet<List<Integer>> ans ){
        
        if( l >= n ){
            List<Integer> p = convertToArrayList(a);
            ans.add( new ArrayList(p) );
            return;
        }
        
        for( int i = l ; i < n ; i++ ){
            
            if( a[i] != a[l] ){
                
                swap( a , l , i);
		            
                permute( l + 1 , n , a , ans );
    		            
                swap( a , l , i);
            }
            else{
                permute( l + 1 , n , a , ans );
            }
            
		            
        }
        
        
        
    }
    
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		// your code goes here
		BufferedReader br = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));

		
		PrintWriter out = new PrintWriter(System.out);
		
// 		int t = sc.nextInt();
	    int t = Integer.valueOf( br.readLine() );
		
		while( t--  > 0 ){
		    int n = Integer.valueOf( br.readLine() );
		    
		    int [] a = new int[n];
		    
		    String s = br.readLine();
		    
		    String str [] = s.split( " " );
		    
		    for (int i = 0 ; i < n ; i++ ) a[i] = Integer.valueOf( str[i] );
		    
		    Arrays.sort( a );
		    
		    HashSet<List<Integer>> ans = new HashSet<>();
		    
		  //  System.out.println( Arrays.toString( a ) );
		  
		    List<Integer> temp = convertToArrayList( a );
		    
		    boolean flag = false;
		    
		    for( int e : temp ){
		        if( Collections.frequency( temp , e ) == n ){
		            flag = true;
		            break;
		        }
		    }
		    
		    if( flag ){
		        
		        out.println( 1 );
		        
		        out.println( temp.toString().replace(",","").replace("[","").replace("]","") );
		        
		    }
		    else{
		        
		        permute( 0 , n , a , ans );
		    
    		    out.println( ans.size() );
    		    
    		    List<List<Integer>> ians = new ArrayList<>(ans);
    		    
    		    Collections.sort( ians , new Comparator<List<Integer>>(){
                    public int compare(List<Integer> list1, List<Integer> list2){
                        int result = 0;
                        for (int i = 0; i <= list1.size() - 1 && result == 0; i++) 
                        {
                            result = list1.get(i).compareTo(list2.get(i));
                        }
                        return result;
                    }
                });
    		    for( List<Integer> b : ians ){
    		        
    		        out.println( b.toString().replace(",","").replace("[","").replace("]","") );
    		        
    		    }
		    }
		    
		}
		
		out.close();
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
    
    static void subset( int a[] ,  HashSet<List<Integer>> set , List<Integer> temp , int i  ){
        
        if( i == a.length ){
            
            if( temp.size() > 0 )set.add( new ArrayList<>(temp) );
            
            return;
            
        }
        
        temp.add( a[i] );
        
        subset( a , set , temp , i + 1 );
        
        temp.remove( temp.size() - 1 );
        
        subset( a , set , temp , i + 1 );
        
    }
    
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		// your code goes here
		Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
		
		int t = sc.nextInt();
		
		while(t-- > 0 ){
		    
		    int n = sc.nextInt();
		    
		    int a[] = new int[n];
		    
		    for (int i = 0 ; i < n ; i++ ) a[i] = sc.nextInt();
		    
		    Arrays.sort( a );
		    
		    HashSet<List<Integer>> set = new HashSet<>();
		    
		    subset( a , set , new ArrayList<>() ,  0 );
		    
		    List<List<Integer>> ians = new ArrayList<>(set);
    		    
    		    Collections.sort( ians , new Comparator<List<Integer>>(){
                    public int compare(List<Integer> list1, List<Integer> list2){
                        int result = 0;
                        int min = Math.min(list1.size(),list2.size());
                        for(int i = 0; i < min; i++) {
                            int compareResult = list1.get(i).compareTo(list2.get(i));
                    
                            if(compareResult != 0) {
                              return compareResult;
                            }
                          }
                        return Integer.compare(list1.size(), list2.size());
                    }
                });
		   
		    
		    System.out.println( ians.size() );
		    
		    for( List<Integer> b : ians ){
		        
		        System.out.println( b.toString().replace( ",","" ).replace("[","").replace("]","") );
		        
		    }
		    
		}
	}
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		// your code goes here
		Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
		int t=sc.nextInt();
		while(t-->0){
		    int n=sc.nextInt();
		    List<String> result = generateParenthesis(n);
		    System.out.println(result.size());
		    for(int i=0;i<result.size();i++){
                System.out.println(result.get(i));
            }
		}
	}
	public static List<String> generateParenthesis(int n) {
        List<String> result = new ArrayList<>();
        generateAll(result, "", 0, 0, n);
        return result;
    }

    private static void generateAll(List<String> result, String current, int open, int close, int max) {
        if (current.length() == 2 * max) {
            result.add(current);
            return;
        }

        if (open < max) {
            generateAll(result, current + "(", open + 1, close, max);
        }

        if (close < open) {
            generateAll(result, current + ")", open, close + 1, max);
        }
    }
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
	   BufferedReader br = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
    BufferedWriter bw = new BufferedWriter(new OutputStreamWriter(System.out));
    int T = Integer.parseInt(br.readLine());
    for (int i=0; i<T; i++) {
      String[] nm = br.readLine().split(" ");
      int   N = Integer.parseInt(nm[0]);
      int   M = Integer.parseInt(nm[1]);
      Graph g = new Graph(N);
      
      for (int edge_no=0; edge_no<M; edge_no++) {
        String[] edge = br.readLine().split(" ");
        int start = Integer.parseInt(edge[0]);
        int end   = Integer.parseInt(edge[1]);
        g.edges[start][end] = g.edges[end][start] = 1;
      }

      g.find_components();
      int Q = Integer.parseInt(br.readLine());
      for (int q=0; q<Q; q++) {
        String[] query = br.readLine().split(" ");
        int A = Integer.parseInt(query[0]);
        int B = Integer.parseInt(query[1]);
        bw.write((g.label[A]==g.label[B])?"YO":"NO");
        bw.newLine();
      }
    }
    bw.close();
    }
}
class Graph {
  int n_nodes;
  int[][] edges;
  int[] label;

  public Graph(int n) {
    this.n_nodes = n;
    this.edges   = new int[n][n];
    this.label   = new int[n];
  }

  public void dfs(int v, int color) {
    label[v] = color;
    for (int neighbor=0; neighbor<n_nodes; neighbor++) {
      if (edges[v][neighbor]==1 && label[neighbor]==0) {
        dfs(neighbor, color);
      }
    }
  }

  public void find_components() {
    int start = 0;
    int comp_no = 1;
    do {
      dfs(start,comp_no);
      comp_no++;
      while(start<n_nodes && label[start]!=0) start++;
    } while (start!=n_nodes);
  }
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
	    Scanner cin = new Scanner(System.in);
        StringBuffer sb = new StringBuffer();
        int n = cin.nextInt();
        while (n-- > 0) {
            int i = cin.nextInt();
            int j = cin.nextInt();
            sb.append(getShortestPathLength(i, j)).append("\n");
        }
        System.out.println(sb);
	}
	private static int getShortestPathLength(int i, int j) {
        ArrayList<Integer> iPath = new ArrayList<Integer>();
        ArrayList<Integer> jPath = new ArrayList<Integer>();

        iPath.add(i);
        jPath.add(j);
        while (i > 0) {
            if (i % 2 == 0) {
                i = (i >> 1);
                iPath.add(i);
            } else {
                i = ((i - 1) >> 1);
                iPath.add(i);
            }
        }
        while (j > 0) {
            if (j % 2 == 0) {
                j = (j >> 1);
                jPath.add(j);
            } else {
                j = ((j - 1) >> 1);
                jPath.add(j);
            }
        }
        Collections.sort(iPath);
        Collections.sort(jPath);
        int len = 0;
        for (int k = iPath.size() - 1; k >= 0; k--) {
            int val = iPath.get(k);
            int l = Collections.binarySearch(jPath, val);
            if (l >= 0) {
                len = jPath.size() - l - 1 + iPath.size() - k - 1;
                break;
            }
        }
        return len;
    }
}

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;

/* Name of the class has to be "Main" only if the class is public. */
class Codechef
{
	public static void main (String[] args) throws java.lang.Exception
	{
		Scanner scn = new Scanner(System.in);
    int t = Integer.parseInt(scn.nextLine());

    ArrayList<ArrayList<int[]>> graph = new ArrayList<>();
    for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) graph.add(new ArrayList<>());

    graph.get(0).add(new int[] { 0, 0 });
    graph.get(0).add(new int[] { 1, 1 });

    graph.get(1).add(new int[] { 1, 1 });
    graph.get(1).add(new int[] { 2, 0 });

    graph.get(2).add(new int[] { 1, 1 });
    graph.get(2).add(new int[] { 3, 0 });

    graph.get(3).add(new int[] { 4, 0 });
    graph.get(3).add(new int[] { 1, 1 });

    graph.get(4).add(new int[] { 0, 0 });
    graph.get(4).add(new int[] { 1, 1 });

    while (t-- != 0) {
      String s = scn.nextLine();
      int node = 0;
      int idx = 0;
      while (idx < s.length()) {
        int val = s.charAt(idx) - '0';
        ArrayList<int[]> nbr = graph.get(node);
        if (val == 0) {
          if (nbr.get(0)[1] == 0) {
            node = nbr.get(0)[0];
          } else {
            node = nbr.get(1)[0];
          }
        } else {
          if (nbr.get(0)[1] == 1) {
            node = nbr.get(0)[0];
          } else {
            node = nbr.get(1)[0];
          }
        }
        idx++;
      }
      if (node == 4) {
        System.out.println("YES");
      } else {
        System.out.println("NO");
      }
    }
	}
}

16/11/2023, 15:52 - Piyush Nayak: Creating a Tcl script for network simulation involves using the Network Simulator (ns-2) and the Network Animator (NAM). Unfortunately, I can't provide you with a complete Tcl script here, but I can give you a basic outline to get you started. Please note that creating a detailed script might require additional considerations based on your specific simulation requirements.

1. **Topology Setup:**
   Define the nodes, links, and their characteristics.

```tcl
# Create a simulator instance
set ns [new Simulator]

# Define nodes
set n0 $ns node
set n1 $ns node
set n2 $ns node

# Create links
$ns duplex-link $n0 $n1 10kb 100ms DropTail
$ns duplex-link $n1 $n2 5mb 200ms DropTail
```

2. **Traffic Generation:**
   Set up traffic from node "n0" to node "n2."

```tcl
# Traffic from n0 to n2
set udp_traffic [new Agent/UDP]
$ns attach-agent $n0 $udp_traffic

set cbr_traffic [new Application/Traffic/CBR]
$cbr_traffic attach-agent $udp_traffic
$cbr_traffic set type_ "cbr"
$cbr_traffic set packet_size_ 1000   ;# Adjust packet size as needed
$cbr_traffic set rate_ 1mbps        ;# Adjust traffic rate as needed

$ns connect $udp_traffic $n2
```

3. **Simulation Configuration:**
   Set simulation parameters and runtime.

```tcl
# Simulation configuration
$ns color 1 Blue   ;# Set color for n0-n1 link
$ns color 2 Red    ;# Set color for n1-n2 link

# Define simulation end time
set simulation_time 5s   ;# Adjust as needed

# Schedule events
$ns at $simulation_time "$ns stop"
```

4. **NAM Configuration:**
   Enable tracing for NAM.

```tcl
# Enable NAM tracing
set nam_file [open out.nam w]
$ns namtrace-all $nam_file
```

5. **Run Simulation:**
   Execute the simulation.

```tcl
# Run the simulation
$ns run
```

Save this script in a file, e.g., `simulation_script.tcl`. Run it using the ns-2 simulator:

```bash
$ ns simulation_script.tcl
```

This script provides a basic framework. Depending on your specific requirements, you might need to adjust parameters, add error models, or customize the traffic patterns. Refer to the ns-2 documentation for detailed information on available modules and configuration options.
